preliminary report and the investigating officers chronological record were the same as those presently used save for word changes made to accommodate court rulings and political correctness reports were the same and bosch decided that homicide investigation was largely the same now as back then of course there had been incredible technological advances in the past thirtyfive years but he believed there were some things that were always the same and always would remain the same the legwork the art of interviewing and listening knowing when to trust an instinct or a hunch those were
